### Candidate 25: Sin-based with exp(P*c4).
sin can't match the needed terms.
**Candidate 25 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

### Candidate 26: `P*c0 + c1*sin(c2*t+c3) + c4*log(P*c5+1) + c6 + c7*exp(c8*t) + c9*t`
Wait - this has exp(c8*t) but not P*exp(c8*t). And sin/log can't match exp(-Î±P).
**Candidate 26 verdict: [NO MATCH]**

1. P (linear)

Most candidates use sin, log, t*exp(ct), rational functions, or power functions - none of which can match exp(-Î±P)*P or P*exp(-Î±t) simultaneously.
